# <a name="obsolete-members-in-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="398ab-102">.NET 框架中的過時成員</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="398ab-102">Obsolete members in .NET Framework</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="398ab-103">本文列出了 .NET Framework 4.5 和更高版本中過時的類型成員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="398ab-103">This article list the type members that are obsolete in .NET Framework 4.5 and later versions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="398ab-104">類型成員按程式集分組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="398ab-104">Type members are grouped by assembly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="398ab-105">本文不會列出過時的類型成員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="398ab-105">This article doesn't list the members of obsolete types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="398ab-106">有關過時型態的清單,請參閱[過時類型](obsolete-types.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="398ab-106">For a list of obsolete types, see [Obsolete types](obsolete-types.md).</span></span>

## <a name="iehostdll-and-ieexecexe"></a><span data-ttu-id="398ab-1108">IEHost.dll 和 IEExec.exe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="398ab-1108">IEHost.dll and IEExec.exe</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="398ab-1109">IEHost.dll 和 IEExec.exe 程式集已從 .NET 框架中刪除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="398ab-1109">The IEHost.dll and IEExec.exe assemblies have been removed from .NET Framework.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="398ab-1110">其所有類型及其成員都已過時,在 .NET 框架 4.5 及更高版本中不受支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="398ab-1110">All of their types and their members are obsolete and are not supported in .NET Framework 4.5 and later.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="398ab-1111">這些組件之前是用來裝載 Windows Form 控制項以及在 Internet Explorer 中執行可執行檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="398ab-1111">These assemblies were used to host Windows Forms controls and to run executables in Internet Explorer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="398ab-1112">這項技術的替代做法包括 ClickOnce、XAML 瀏覽器應用程式 (XBAP) 和 Microsoft Silverlight。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="398ab-1112">Alternatives to this technology include ClickOnce, XAML Browser Applications (XBAP), and Microsoft Silverlight.</span></span>
